kind: GrafanaDatasource
metadata:
  name: grafana-datasource
  namespace: monitoring
spec:
  allowCrossNamespaceImport: true
  valuesFrom:
    - targetPath: "secureJsonData.httpHeaderValue1"
      valueFrom:
        secretKeyRef:
          name: grafana-sa-token
          key: token
  instanceSelector:
    matchLabels:
      dashboards: grafana
  datasource:
    name: Prometheus
    type: prometheus
    access: proxy
    url: https://thanos-querier.openshift-monitoring.svc:9091
    isDefault: true
    jsonData:
      tlsSkipVerify: true
      timeInterval: "5s"
      httpHeaderName1: "Authorization"
    secureJsonData:
      httpHeaderValue1: "Bearer ${token}"

######## FILE: ./fraud-platform/k8s/fraud-exporter/deployment.yaml ########
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: fraud-metrics-exporter
  namespace: kafka
  labels:
    app: fraud-metrics-exporter
spec:
  replicas: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: fraud-metrics-exporter
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: fraud-metrics-exporter
      annotations:
        prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
        prometheus.io/port: "9090"
        prometheus.io/path: "/metrics"
    spec:
      containers:
        - name: exporter
          image: image-registry.openshift-image-registry.svc:5000/kafka/fraud-metrics-exporter:latest
          imagePullPolicy: Always
          ports:
            - containerPort: 9090
          resources:
            requests:
              cpu: 50m
              memory: 64Mi
            limits:
              cpu: 200m
              memory: 128Mi
          livenessProbe:
            httpGet:
              path: /health
              port: 9090
            initialDelaySeconds: 30
            periodSeconds: 30
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: fraud-metrics-exporter
  namespace: kafka
  labels:
    app: fraud-metrics-exporter
spec:
  selector:
    app: fraud-metrics-exporter
  ports:
    - port: 9090
      targetPort: 9090
      name: metrics

######## FILE: ./fraud-platform/k8s/fraud-exporter/servicemonitor.yaml ########
apiVersion: monitoring.coreos.com/v1
kind: ServiceMonitor
metadata:
  name: fraud-metrics-exporter
  namespace: kafka
  labels:
    app: fraud-metrics-exporter
spec:
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: fraud-metrics-exporter
  endpoints:
    - port: metrics
      interval: 60s
      path: /metrics

  - deployment.yaml
  - servicemonitor.yaml
